On Swami Vivekananda's 160th Jayanti (12th Jan 2022), Think India /VSS is organizing a talk with retired major general G.D.Bakshi. 

 

Major General Gagan Deep Bakshi or G.D. Bakshi retired major general of Indian army will be speaking about late CDS Bipin Rawat, renowned Indian military officer, India’s first chief of defence staff and who has also served as Indian army chief, but unfortunately, he died recently due to a fatal helicopter crash. CDS Bipin Rawat is a lost gem of India and his life in itself is too inspiring. 

 So don’t miss this opportunity to be a part of such an insightful and motivational session where you will come to know about this legend closely.

[27/01/22, 12:56:19 AM] Nehal ECE: Step 1: The application process

This one is easy. What you have to do is set up a date - with a friend, with a partner, your pet, someone from your family or just yourself.


Have fun on the date.

Make a reel out of it.

Share it.


Here’s this broken down into 5 simple steps:

Set up the date and make the reel
Share it on 1st February, 5pm
Tag @mingoutsocial and use the hashtag #1becomes2
On 2nd February, at 5pm, send a screenshot of the reel views to maya@mingout.in
Wait for your reward :)

What’s in it for you?

The top 100 reels get 2 free passes for the artist of their choice on the Mingout Valentine’s fest + a certificate of appreciation.
Top 20 reels get 5 free passes for the artist of their choice on the Mingout Valentine’s fest + a certificate of achievement.
Top 10 individuals get selected for the summer/term internship with stipend ranging from INR 25,000 to INR 50,000/month + letter of recommendations from the founders

Artists for the Mingout Valentines fest are likely to include:

Prateek Kuhad, Urooj Ashfaq, Anuv Jain, Osho Jain, Rahul Dua, Vishnu Kaushal among others.

Apart from the passes, we might be able to get you personal 1 on 1s with your favorite artists. But we don’t want to promise what we can’t deliver. This is a possibility, not a commitment :)


If this sounds interesting, please sign up through the form below.


Internship Application Form


Step 2: The internship


What happens to selected applications?

At least 10 applicants will be selected for a live project/summer internship/in-sem internship (as per availability of student) in the CEO’s office. The roles are akin to growth roles at firms

1 week of orientation
2 weeks of rotation
Remainder of the time period in 1 role within the organisation, from the below
Brand and communications
Events and artist management
Design and product
Growth and strategy
Digital marketing

Stipend: Between INR 25,000 to INR 50,000 / month


We will also launch the Mingout College Ambassador program at the beginning of the next academic year. Applicants for this internship will be given preference for the same.

The celebrations of Republic Day are special this year as India is in the 75th year of Independence - being celebrated as 'Azadi ka Amrit Mahotsav'. 
To mark the occasion, we invite you to participate in this fun-filled interactive session on 'An Inclusive India' to further the spirit of tolerance and inclusiveness.

DATE: 29 January 2022 (Saturday)
TIME: 5.00 pm onwards
REGISTRATION LINK: https://shrtco.de/ZNLwyb

Our college exhibits the true essence of multiculturalism. Keeping up with this spirit, we invite your ideas on:
- Changing cultural trends and youth
- Stereotypes that infuriate you the most
- Part you can play in changing preconceived notions
- Role of government and society in constructing and deconstructing perceptions

This will be followed by a fun activity on shattering stereotypes. Make sure to have a paper/balloon and a pen close by.

The most active and convincing participants will be rewarded with a Certificate of Appreciation!
Do join for lots of fun and togetherness!

[27/04/22, 3:09:52 PM] ‪+91 82733 15253‬: #include <reg51.h>

void transmitData(char ch) {
	SBUF = ch;	
	while (!TI);	
	TI = 0;		
}

void String(char *str) {
	int i;
	for(i=0;str[i]!='\0';i++)	/* Send each char of string till the NULL */
		transmitData(str[i]);
}

void main() {

	// Timer 1, 8-bit auto reload mode
	TMOD = 0x20;
	
	// Load value for 9600 baud rate
	TH1 = 0xFD;	
	
	// Mode 1, reception enable
	SCON = 0x50;		
	
	// Start timer 1
	TR1 = 1;

	String("CAPPUCCINO");	

	while(1);
}

[05/05/22, 1:50:19 PM] Ankit Ece: #include<reg51.h>

// PWM_Pin
sbit PWM_Pin = P2^0;		   // Pin P2.0 is named as PWM_Pin

// Function declarations
void cct_init(void);
void InitTimer0(void);
void InitPWM(void);

// Global variables
unsigned char PWM = 0;	  // It can have a value from 0 (0% duty cycle) to 255 (100% duty cycle)
unsigned int temp = 0;    // Used inside Timer0 ISR

// PWM frequency selector
/* PWM_Freq_Num can have values in between 1 to 257	only
 * When PWM_Freq_Num is equal to 1, then it means highest PWM frequency
 * which is approximately 1000000/(1*255) = 3.9kHz
 * When PWM_Freq_Num is equal to 257, then it means lowest PWM frequency
 * which is approximately 1000000/(257*255) = 15Hz
 *
 * So, in general you can calculate PWM frequency by using the formula
 *     PWM Frequency = 1000000/(PWM_Freq_Num*255)
 */
#define PWM_Freq_Num   1	 // Highest possible PWM Frequency


// Main Function
int main(void)
{
   cct_init();   	       // Make all ports zero
   InitPWM();              // Start PWM
 
   PWM = 127;              // Make 50% duty cycle of PWM

   while(1)                // Rest is done in Timer0 interrupt
   {}
}

// Init CCT function
void cct_init(void)
{
	P0 = 0x00;   
	P1 = 0x00;   
	P2 = 0x00;   
	P3 = 0x00;  
}

// Timer0 initialize
void InitTimer0(void)
{
	TMOD &= 0xF0;    // Clear 4bit field for timer0
	TMOD |= 0x01;    // Set timer0 in mode 1 = 16bit mode
	
	TH0 = 0x00;      // First time value
	TL0 = 0x00;      // Set arbitrarily zero
	
	ET0 = 1;         // Enable Timer0 interrupts
	EA  = 1;         // Global interrupt enable
	
	TR0 = 1;         // Start Timer 0
}

// PWM initialize
void InitPWM(void)
{
	PWM = 0;         // Initialize with 0% duty cycle
	InitTimer0();    // Initialize timer0 to start generating interrupts
					 // PWM generation code is written inside the Timer0 ISR
}

// Timer0 ISR
void Timer0_ISR (void) interrupt 1   
{
	TR0 = 0;    // Stop Timer 0

	if(PWM_Pin)	// if PWM_Pin is high
	{
		PWM_Pin = 0;
		temp = (255-PWM)*PWM_Freq_Num;
		TH0  = 0xFF - (temp>>8)&0xFF;
		TL0  = 0xFF - temp&0xFF;	
	}
	else	     // if PWM_Pin is low
	{
		PWM_Pin = 1;
		temp = PWM*PWM_Freq_Num;
		TH0  = 0xFF - (temp>>8)&0xFF;
		TL0  = 0xFF - temp&0xFF;
	}

	TF0 = 0;     // Clear the interrupt flag
	TR0 = 1;     // Start Timer 0
}

[28/12/22, 12:27:23 AM] Nehal ECE: Job Description: Front End Intern 

We are a growing SaaS startup looking for talented and passionate Full Stack Interns to join our team. In this role, you will work closely with our founders for our web-based SaaS applications.

As a Front End Intern , you will be responsible for:


* Developing and implementing user-facing features using modern front-end technologies, such as HTML, CSS, and JavaScript
* Collaborating with the design team to create visually appealing and user-friendly interfaces
* Writing clean, maintainable, and well-documented code
* Participating in code reviews and providing feedback to other team members
* Troubleshooting and debugging front-end issues
* Keeping up to date with the latest front-end technologies and best practices


To be successful in this role, you should have:


* A passion for front-end development and user experience
* Strong proficiency in HTML, CSS, and JavaScript
* Experience with modern front-end frameworks, such as React 
* Good understanding of web accessibility standards
* Excellent communication and collaboration skills
* This is a full-time internship position and will be based remotely. We offer competitive compensation and benefits, as well as opportunities for growth and development within the company.


If you are interested in working at the forefront of SaaS and front-end development, and are eager to learn and grow with a dynamic startup, we would love to hear from you. Please submit your resume to apply for this position. We are open to you working part-time along with your college.

Please feel free to connect at +91-8090868880
